      var timestamp
      var result

window.Images = (function (window, document, undefined) {
  'use strict'

  /** @type {string} */
  var _successClass = 'lazy-image--loaded'

  /** @type {string} */
  var _errorClass = 'lazy-image--error'

  /** @type {array} */
  var _breakpoints = ['xs', 'sm', 'md', 'lg', 'xl']

  /** @type {object} */
  var _this

  return {
    /**
     * We check async if the browser supports one of the newer formats (webp, jpeg2000) and store it here.
     * To only perform the async tests once we store it in the sessionStorage of the browser.
     * @type {string}
     */
    /* _modernFormat: Modernizr.sessionstorage ? sessionStorage.getItem('modernFormat') || '' : '', */
    _modernFormat: '',

    /**
     * Here we store all the image containers. Once they're loaded, they get removed from here and added to _loadedImageContainers.
     * @type {array}
     */
    _imageContainers: [],

    /**
     * Whether we should use lazyload or deferred loading (fallback)
     * @type {boolean}
     */
    lazyLoadImages: true,

    /**
     * Here we store all the LOADED image containers. Gets flushed on breakpoint change.
     * @type {array}
     */
    _loadedImageContainers: [],

    /** @function */
    init: function () {
      _this = window.Images
      _this.defineRequestAnimationFrame()
      _this.events.init()
      _this.lazyLoadImages = (Utils.currentBreakpoint.name !== 'xs' &amp;&amp; Utils.currentBreakpoint.name !== 'sm')

      var imageElements = document.querySelectorAll('.lazy-image')
      for (var i = 0, length = imageElements.length; i &lt; length; i++) {
        !Utils.parents(imageElements[i], '.carousel') &amp;&amp; _this.add(imageElements[i])
      }
    },

    /**
     * @type {object}
     * @property {function} init - Bind general events
     */
    events: {
      init: function () {
        window.addEventListener('breakpointChange', _this.onBreakpointChange)
        document.getElementById('lightbox') &amp;&amp; document.getElementById('lightbox').addEventListener('scroll', Utils.debounce(_this.update, 200))
        window.addEventListener('scroll', Utils.debounce(_this.update, 200))
      }
    },

    /** @function */
    defineRequestAnimationFrame: function () {
      window.requestAnimationFrame = (function () {
        return window.requestAnimationFrame ||
                    window.webkitRequestAnimationFrame ||
                    window.mozRequestAnimationFrame ||
                    window.msRequestAnimationFrame ||
                    function (callback) { return window.setTimeout(callback, 0) }
      })()

      window.cancelAnimationFrame = (function () {
        return window.cancelAnimationFrame ||
                    window.webkitCancelAnimationFrame ||
                    window.mozCancelAnimationFrame ||
                    window.msCancelAnimationFrame ||
                    function (intervalKey) { window.clearTimeout(intervalKey) }
      })()
    },

    isVisible: function (elem) {
      return !!(elem.offsetWidth || elem.offsetHeight || elem.getClientRects().length)
    },

    /**
     * We need to refill the _loadedImageContainers onBreakpointChange due to the fact that
     * the already loaded container could have a different ressource for the new breakpoint.
     * That's why we merge the two arrays and then flush _loadedImageContainers to fill it up again.
     * Then check if we need to load something new instantly.
     * Aftewards the update method takes over (e.g. during scrolling) and executes similar logic.
     */
    onBreakpointChange: function () {
      Array.prototype.push.apply(_this._imageContainers, _this._loadedImageContainers)
      _this._loadedImageContainers = []

      var tempImageContainers = []
      for (var i = 0, length = _this._imageContainers.length; i &lt; length; i++) {
        var container = _this._imageContainers[i]
        _this.setCorrectSrc(container)

        if (!container.loaded &amp;&amp; Utils.isVisible(container.container)) {
          _this.loadImage(container)
          _this._loadedImageContainers.push(container)
        } else if (container.loaded) {
          _this._loadedImageContainers.push(container)
        } else {
          tempImageContainers.push(container)
        }
      }
      _this._imageContainers = tempImageContainers
    },

    /**
     * Add image container that should be observed
     * @param {jQuery} $el - Can be one or multiple elements
     * @param {boolean} temporary - Marks images that can be deleted at some point
     */
    add: function (el, temporary) {
      if (el.length) {
        for (var i = 0, length = el.length; i &lt; length; i++) {
          _this.add(el[i], temporary)
        }

        return this
      }

      var container = {
        container: el,
        img: el.querySelector('img') !== null ? el.querySelector('img') : el,
        lazyLoad: el.classList ? el.classList.contains('lazy-image') : el.className.indexOf('lazy-image') !== -1,
        loaded: el.classList ? !el.classList.contains('lazy-image') : el.className.indexOf('lazy-image') === -1,
        currentSrc: '',
        currentQueryString: '',
        temporary: !!temporary
      }

      /** Store max dimensions */
      container.maxWidth = container.img.getAttribute('data-originalimagewidth') || null
      container.maxHeight = container.img.getAttribute('data-originalimageheight') || null

      var j = _breakpoints.length
      var src

      /** Get source and queryString for each data-src-x attribute and store it as a separate object */
      while (j--) {
        if (container.img.getAttribute('data-src-' + _breakpoints[j])) {
          src = container.img.getAttribute('data-src-' + _breakpoints[j])

          if (src.indexOf('?') !== -1) {
            container[_breakpoints[j]] = {
              src: src.substring(0, src.indexOf('?')),
              queryString: src.substring(src.indexOf('?'))
            }
          } else {
            /** Some images don't have a querystring. Just use the normal src in this case. */
            container[_breakpoints[j]] = {
              src: src,
              queryString: ''
            }
          }
        }
      }

      src = container.img.getAttribute('data-src') || ''

      if (src.indexOf('?') !== -1) {
        container.src = src.substring(0, src.indexOf('?'))
        container.queryString = src.substring(src.indexOf('?'))
      } else {
        /** Some images don't have a querystring. Just use the normal src in this case. */
        container.src = src
        container.queryString = ''
      }

      _this._imageContainers.push(container)

      return this
    },

    /**
     * Checks each container for its visibility.
     * If it's visible but no image was loaded yet, load it and remove the container from the store (_imageContainers).
     * This way we don't have to loop each container every time and therefore save memory usage.
     */
    update: function () {
      if (!_this._imageContainers.length || !window.navigator.onLine) {
        return
      }

      if (!_this.lazyLoadImages) {
        requestAnimationFrame(function () {
          var images = document.querySelectorAll('.lazy-image:not(.lazy-image--loaded)')
          for (var i = 0, length = images.length; i &lt; length; i++) {
            if (_this.isVisible(images[i])) {
              _this.show(images[i])
            }
          }
        })
        return
      }

      var tempImageContainers = []
      for (var i = 0, length = _this._imageContainers.length; i &lt; length; i++) {
        var container = _this._imageContainers[i]

        if (!document.body.contains(container.container)) {
          _this._loadedImageContainers.push(container)
          container.loaded = true
        } else {
          if (!container.loaded &amp;&amp; Utils.isVisible(container.container)) {
            _this.setCorrectSrc(container)
            _this._loadedImageContainers.push(container)
            _this.loadImage(container)
          } else if (!container.loaded) {
            tempImageContainers.push(container)
          }
        }
      }
      _this._imageContainers = tempImageContainers
    },

    /**
     * Method to force an element to load and appear (even if it isn't currently visible to the user).
     * @param $el {jQuery}
     */
    show: function (el) {
      var length
      var i

      if (el.length) {
        length = el.length

        for (i = 0; i &lt; length; i++) {
          _this.show(el[i])
        }

        return this
      }

      var container
      length = _this._imageContainers.length

      /** Get correct object and remove it from the storage */
      for (i = 0; i &lt; length; i++) {
        var obj = _this._imageContainers[i]
        if (obj.container === el) {
          container = obj
          _this._imageContainers.splice(i, 1)
          break
        }
      }

      if (!!container &amp;&amp; !container.loaded) {
        _this.setCorrectSrc(container)
        _this.loadImage(container)
        _this._loadedImageContainers.push(container)
      }
    },

    /** @param {object} container */
    loadImage: function (container) {
      if (container.currentSrc) {
        var src = container.currentSrc
        var url = src + _this.getCorrectQueryString(container, _this._modernFormat)
        var tmpImg = new Image()

        url = _this._modernFormat ? url.replace('progressive-jpeg', _this._modernFormat) : url

        tmpImg.onerror = function () {
          if (container.container.classList) {
            container.container.classList.add(_errorClass)
          } else {
            container.container.className += ' ' + _errorClass
          }
        }

        tmpImg.onload = function () {
          var img = container.img

          /* Is element an image or should we add the src as a background image? */
          if (img.tagName === 'IMG') {
            img.setAttribute('src', url)
          } else {
            img.style['background-image'] = 'url("' + url + '")'
          }
          container.loaded = true
          container.currentSrc = src

          if (container.container.classList) {
            container.container.classList.add(_successClass)
          } else {
            container.container.className += ' ' + _successClass
          }

          var event = document.createEvent('CustomEvent')
          event.initCustomEvent('imageLoaded', true, true, {})

          container.container.dispatchEvent(event)
        }

        tmpImg.src = url
      }
    },

    /**
     * Check if we need to change the source depeneding on the current active breakpoint.
     * A "higher" breakpoint has priority over a "lower".
     * E.g. if the current active breakpoint is "xl", the source for "lg" has priority over the one for "md".
     * @param {object} container
     */
    setCorrectSrc: function (container) {
      var newBreakpoint = container

      if (container[Utils.currentBreakpoint.name]) {
        newBreakpoint = container[Utils.currentBreakpoint.name]
      } else if (Utils.currentBreakpoint.name === 'xl') {
        if (container.lg) {
          newBreakpoint = container.lg
        } else if (container.md) {
          newBreakpoint = container.md
        } else if (container.sm) {
          newBreakpoint = container.sm
        } else if (container.xs) {
          newBreakpoint = container.xs
        }
      } else if (Utils.currentBreakpoint.name === 'lg') {
        if (container.md) {
          newBreakpoint = container.md
        } else if (container.sm) {
          newBreakpoint = container.sm
        } else if (container.xs) {
          newBreakpoint = container.xs
        }
      } else if (Utils.currentBreakpoint.name === 'md') {
        if (container.sm) {
          newBreakpoint = container.sm
        } else if (container.xs) {
          newBreakpoint = container.xs
        }
      } else if (Utils.currentBreakpoint.name === 'sm' &amp;&amp; container.xs) {
        newBreakpoint = container.xs
      }

      if (newBreakpoint.src !== container.currentSrc) {
        container.currentSrc = newBreakpoint.src
        container.currentQueryString = newBreakpoint.queryString
        container.loaded = false
      }
    },

    /** @param {object} $container */
    getCorrectQueryString: function (container, modernformat) {
      /** Return empty string for cases when there is no query string */
      if (!container.currentQueryString) {
        return ''
      }

      var cWidth = Utils.retina ? container.container.clientWidth * 2 : container.container.clientWidth
      var cHeight = Utils.retina ? container.container.clientHeight * 2 : container.container.clientHeight

      /** +3 because of the encoded pipe symbol */
      var start = container.currentQueryString.indexOf('fit=inside') + 'fit=inside'.length + 3
      var end = container.currentQueryString.indexOf('&amp;output-format')
      var dimensions = {
        width: cWidth,
        height: cHeight
      }
      var imgDataHeight = container.container.getAttribute('data-height')

      /**
             * Fix for JPEG2000 blurry images in cases where the request comes from a touch device and
             * the defined image size is smaller then 100px. If the defined image size is 0, it
             * will not be changed because 0 is handled like 100% for bigger images.
             */
      if (modernformat === 'jpeg2000') {
        var fixedSize = 100
        var width = cWidth &lt; fixedSize &amp;&amp; cWidth !== 0 ? fixedSize : cWidth
        var height = cHeight &lt; fixedSize &amp;&amp; cHeight !== 0 ? fixedSize : cHeight

        dimensions = {
          width: width,
          height: height
        }
      }

      /**
       * We need some special logic for teasers as they are fully fluid for breakpoints &lt;= sm and
       * therefore can have plenty of diffrent widths.
       */
      if (Utils.parents(container.container, '.promo-teaser')) {
        if (Utils.currentBreakpoint.name === 'xs') {
          dimensions.width = Utils.currentBreakpoint.max
          dimensions.height = Utils.currentBreakpoint.max / 2
        } else if (Utils.currentBreakpoint.name === 'sm') {
          dimensions.width = Utils.currentBreakpoint.max
          dimensions.height = 'h'
        } else if (Utils.currentBreakpoint.name === 'md' &amp;&amp; Utils.parents(container.container, '#additional-area')) {
          dimensions.width = Utils.currentBreakpoint.min
          dimensions.height = 'h'
        }
      }

      if (imgDataHeight === 'auto') {
        dimensions.height = 'h'
      }

      if (typeof dimensions.width === 'number' &amp;&amp; container.maxWidth &amp;&amp; dimensions.width &gt; container.maxWidth) {
        dimensions.width = container.maxWidth
      }

      if (typeof dimensions.height === 'number' &amp;&amp; container.maxHeight &amp;&amp; dimensions.height &gt; container.maxHeight) {
        dimensions.height = container.maxHeight
      }

      dimensions = dimensions.width + ':' + dimensions.height

      return container.currentQueryString.replace(container.currentQueryString.slice(start, end), dimensions)
    },

    /** @function */
    removeTemporaryImages: function () {
      var i = 0
      var j = 0

      while (i &lt; _this._imageContainers.length || j &lt; _this._loadedImageContainers.length) {
        if (i &lt; _this._imageContainers.length) {
          if (_this._imageContainers[i].temporary) {
            _this._imageContainers.splice(i, 1)
          } else {
            i++
          }
        }

        if (j &lt; _this._loadedImageContainers.length) {
          if (_this._loadedImageContainers[j].temporary) {
            _this._loadedImageContainers.splice(j, 1)
          } else {
            j++
          }
        }
      }
    }
  }
})(window, document)

document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function () {
  Images.init()
})

window.addEventListener('load', Images.update)

window.addEventListener('load', function () {
    setTimeout(function () {
        if (typeof measurePerformance === 'function') {
            window.measurePerformance()
        }
    }, 0)
})

t=getOwn(S,e.id);t&amp;&amp;!t.enabled&amp;&amp;q.enable(e,this)})),this.enabling=!1,this.check()},on:function(e,t){var i=this.events[e];i||(i=this.events[e]=[]),i.push(t)},emit:function(e,t){each(this.events[e],function(e){e(t)}),"error"===e&amp;&amp;delete
